qt-examples in Fedora 32

This page displays detailed information for a specific version of qt-examples. You might want go back to the main page of qt-examples.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2020-01-31 Than Ngo - 4.8.7-52 - fixed FTBFS against gcc10
2020-01-30 Fedora Release Engineering - 1:4.8.7-51 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_32_Mass_Rebuild

2019-04-02 Rex Dieter - 4.8.7-48 - rebuild
2019-03-22 Than Ngo - 4.8.7-47 - fixed #1691638 - CVE-2018-19872 qt: malformed PPM image causing division by zero and crash in qppmhandler.cpp
2019-02-28 Rex Dieter - 1:4.8.7-46 - backport qforeach.patch from qt5 - -no-javascript-jit on f30 to workaround gcc9 FTBFS for now
2019-02-02 Fedora Release Engineering - 1:4.8.7-45 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_30_Mass_Rebuild
